<script type="text/javascript">
            window._nslDOMReady = (function () {
                const executedCallbacks = new Set();
            
                return function (callback) {
                    /**
                    * Third parties might dispatch DOMContentLoaded events, so we need to ensure that we only run our callback once!
                    */
                    if (executedCallbacks.has(callback)) return;
            
                    const wrappedCallback = function () {
                        if (executedCallbacks.has(callback)) return;
                        executedCallbacks.add(callback);
                        callback();
                    };
            
                    if (document.readyState === "complete" || document.readyState === "interactive") {
                        wrappedCallback();
                    } else {
                        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", wrappedCallback);
                    }
                };
            })();
        </script><script type="text/javascript" src="https://mapyourtech.com/wp-includes/js/dist/hooks.min.js?ver=dd5603f07f9220ed27f1" id="wp-hooks-js"></script>

                    var tc_style = document.createElement("style");

        <script>
        // Method 4: JavaScript solution - Most reliable for any setup
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Find all menu links
            var menuLinks = document.querySelectorAll('nav a, .menu a, #menu a, .nav a');
            
            menuLinks.forEach(function(link) {
                var href = link.getAttribute('href') || '';
                var text = link.textContent.toLowerCase();
                
                // Check for Interview Insights
                if (text.includes('interview') && text.includes('insights')) {
                    addPROTag(link);
                }
                
                // Check for Salary Insights
                if (text.includes('salary') && text.includes('insights')) {
                    addPROTag(link);
                }
                
                // Check by URL patterns
                if (href.includes('25296') || href.includes('25297') || 
                    href.includes('interview-insights') || href.includes('salary-insights')) {
                    addPROTag(link);
                }
            });
            
            function addPROTag(link) {
                // Remove any existing tags
                var existingTag = link.querySelector('.myt-pro-tag');
                if (existingTag) existingTag.remove();
                
                // Create PRO tag
                var proTag = document.createElement('span');
                proTag.className = 'myt-pro-tag';
                proTag.style.cssText = `
                    font-size: 8px !important;
                    background: linear-gradient(135deg, #8e44ad, #3742fa) !important;
                    color: white !important;
                    padding: 2px 6px !important;
                    border-radius: 4px !important;
                    margin-left: 8px !important;
                    vertical-align: super !important;
                    font-weight: 800 !important;
                    text-transform: uppercase !important;
                    letter-spacing: 1px !important;
                    display: inline-block !important;
                    line-height: 1 !important;
                    box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(142, 68, 173, 0.5) !important;
                    border: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.4) !important;
                    animation: myt-pro-shine 2s infinite !important;
                `;
                proTag.textContent = 'PRO';
                
                // Append to link
                link.appendChild(proTag);
                
                console.log('✅ Added PRO tag to:', link.textContent);
            }
        });
        </script>

    <script>
        (function() {
            var animated = false;

            function easeOutQuart(t) {
                return 1 - Math.pow(1 - t, 4);
            }

            function animateCounter(el) {
                var target = parseInt(el.getAttribute('data-target'));
                var duration = target <= 10 ? 1000 : 2000;
                var start = performance.now();

                function tick(now) {
                    var elapsed = now - start;
                    var progress = Math.min(elapsed / duration, 1);
                    var val = Math.floor(easeOutQuart(progress) * target);
                    el.textContent = val;

                    if (progress < 1) {
                        requestAnimationFrame(tick);
                    } else {
                        el.textContent = target;
                        el.style.transform = 'scale(1.12)';
                        el.style.color = '#ff6b00';
                        setTimeout(function() {
                            el.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
                            el.style.color = '#fbbf24';
                        }, 200);
                    }
                }

                requestAnimationFrame(tick);
            }

            function startAllCounters() {
                if (animated) return;
                animated = true;

                var counters = document.querySelectorAll('.myt-stat-number[data-target]');
                for (var i = 0; i < counters.length; i++) {
                    (function(index) {
                        setTimeout(function() {
                            animateCounter(counters[index]);
                        }, index * 200);
                    })(i);
                }
            }

            function init() {
                var section = document.querySelector('.myt-stats-wrapper');
                if (!section) return;

                if ('IntersectionObserver' in window) {
                    var observer = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
                        for (var j = 0; j < entries.length; j++) {
                            if (entries[j].isIntersecting) {
                                startAllCounters();
                                observer.disconnect();
                            }
                        }
                    }, { threshold: 0.2 });
                    observer.observe(section);
                } else {
                    setTimeout(startAllCounters, 1500);
                }
            }

            if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
            } else {
                init();
            }
        })();
    </script>

}
function mytwOpen3(key){

});

mb.appendChild(g);
}
P.classList.add('myt-active');document.body.style.overflow='hidden';
}

<script>
(function() {
    var currentSlide = 0;
    var track = document.getElementById('carouselTrack');
    var cards = track.querySelectorAll('.myt-review-card');
    var indicatorContainer = document.getElementById('carouselIndicators');
    var cardsPerView = 3;
    var autoSlideInterval;

    function getCardsPerView() {
        if (window.innerWidth <= 768) return 1;
        if (window.innerWidth <= 1024) return 2;
        return 3;
    }

    function getTotalSlides() {
        return Math.ceil(cards.length / cardsPerView);
    }

    function buildIndicators() {
        indicatorContainer.innerHTML = '';
        var total = getTotalSlides();
        for (var i = 0; i < total; i++) {
            var dot = document.createElement('span');
            dot.className = 'myt-indicator' + (i === currentSlide ? ' active' : '');
            dot.setAttribute('data-slide', i);
            dot.addEventListener('click', function() {
                goToSlide(parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-slide')));
            });
            indicatorContainer.appendChild(dot);
        }
    }

    function updateCarousel() {
        if (!cards.length) return;
        var cardWidth = cards[0].offsetWidth;
        var gap = 22;
        var offset = currentSlide * cardsPerView * (cardWidth + gap);
        track.style.transform = 'translateX(-' + offset + 'px)';
        
        var dots = indicatorContainer.querySelectorAll('.myt-indicator');
        for (var i = 0; i < dots.length; i++) {
            if (i === currentSlide) {
                dots[i].classList.add('active');
            } else {
                dots[i].classList.remove('active');
            }
        }
    }

    function moveCarousel(direction) {
        var total = getTotalSlides();
        currentSlide += direction;
        if (currentSlide < 0) currentSlide = total - 1;
        if (currentSlide >= total) currentSlide = 0;
        updateCarousel();
        resetAutoSlide();
    }

    function goToSlide(index) {
        currentSlide = index;
        updateCarousel();
        resetAutoSlide();
    }

    function startAutoSlide() {
        autoSlideInterval = setInterval(function() {
            moveCarousel(1);
        }, 5000);
    }

    function resetAutoSlide() {
        clearInterval(autoSlideInterval);
        startAutoSlide();
    }

    window.moveCarousel = moveCarousel;

    cardsPerView = getCardsPerView();
    buildIndicators();
    updateCarousel();
    startAutoSlide();

    var resizeTimer;
    window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
        clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
        resizeTimer = setTimeout(function() {
            var newCpv = getCardsPerView();
            if (newCpv !== cardsPerView) {
                cardsPerView = newCpv;
                currentSlide = 0;
                buildIndicators();
            }
            updateCarousel();
        }, 150);
    });

    var wrapper = document.querySelector('.myt-carousel-wrapper');
    if (wrapper) {
        wrapper.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() { clearInterval(autoSlideInterval); });
        wrapper.addEventListener('mouseleave', startAutoSlide);
    }
})();
</script>

<div class="faq">
    <h2>Common Questions</h2>
    <p class="faq-sub">Everything you need to know before getting started</p>
    <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">What is the difference between Premium and Premium Pro?<svg viewbox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><polyline points="6 9 12 15 18 9"></polyline></svg></div>
        <div class="faq-a">Premium unlocks the full learning and engineering toolkit &mdash; all courses, exclusive articles, professional simulators and calculators, market research reports, and LinkedIn-shareable certificates. Premium Pro adds professional-grade design tools (OptiMap Pro, GOSNR Simulator, GuardBand Pro), career intelligence (interview and salary insights from optical companies), the complete MapYourTech book library, and priority support.</div>
    </div>
    <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">How does the $3 / 48-hour trial work?<svg viewbox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><polyline points="6 9 12 15 18 9"></polyline></svg></div>
        <div class="faq-a">Pay $3 once and get full Premium Pro access for 48 hours &mdash; every course, tool, simulator, and resource. No auto-renewal, no commitment. If you like what you see, you can subscribe to a monthly or annual plan afterward.</div>
    </div>
    <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">I can ask ChatGPT, Claude, or Gemini for free &mdash; why would I pay for this?<svg viewbox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><polyline points="6 9 12 15 18 9"></polyline></svg></div>
        <div class="faq-a">Fair question &mdash; and we encourage you to test it. Ask any AI chatbot to calculate OSNR for a 10-span link with specific amplifier noise figures and see what you get. Or ask it for the correct OTU4 frame overhead byte assignments. You will likely get a confident answer that is partially or completely wrong. AI tools are great for general explanations, but optical networking requires exact values, real-world parameters, and validated calculations. MapYourTech content is written and cross-checked by engineers who design and deploy live networks. Our simulators use actual component specifications &mdash; not approximations. When you are writing a design proposal, presenting to a customer, or troubleshooting at 2 AM, you need answers you can trust without second-guessing. That is what you are paying for.</div>
    </div>
    <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">What do I get here that AI answers and YouTube videos cannot give me?<svg viewbox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><polyline points="6 9 12 15 18 9"></polyline></svg></div>
        <div class="faq-a">AI gives you a fragment. MapYourTech gives you the full engineering loop. Take any topic &mdash; say, ROADM architecture. AI will give you a textbook-level overview. Here, you get the complete picture: what it is, why it matters, how it works at the component level, when to choose CDC-F versus fixed-grid, the real trade-offs between cost and flexibility, field deployment considerations vendors do not document, and interactive simulators where you can model your own network scenarios. Every article is structured from fundamentals through advanced design decisions, written from 18+ years of hands-on experience across live operator networks. AI also cannot tell you what actually happens when you put Vendor A transponders on Vendor B line systems, or why your OSNR margin disappears on aged fiber &mdash; because that knowledge does not exist in any training dataset. It comes from engineers who have been on site, traced the fault, and solved the problem. That structured, experience-backed, full-context learning is what makes the difference between reading about a technology and actually being able to deploy it.</div>
    </div>
    <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">Can I switch plans or cancel anytime?<svg viewbox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><polyline points="6 9 12 15 18 9"></polyline></svg></div>
        <div class="faq-a">Yes. Upgrade, downgrade, or cancel from your account settings at any time. No long-term contracts. If you cancel, you keep access until the end of your billing period.</div>
    </div>
    <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">Will this help me advance my optical networking career?<svg viewbox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><polyline points="6 9 12 15 18 9"></polyline></svg></div>
        <div class="faq-a">MapYourTech is built around how optical networking careers actually grow. The platform covers the full technology spectrum &mdash; from DWDM fundamentals and OTN architecture to 800G coherent design, submarine systems, C+L band engineering, and network automation. But the real difference is that content evolves with the industry. As new standards emerge from ITU-T, OIF, or OpenROADM, and as operators adopt new technologies like coherent pluggables or open line systems, we update courses, articles, and tools to match what engineers need right now &mdash; not what was relevant three years ago. Premium Pro members also get career intelligence that does not exist anywhere else: interview insights and salary data from real optical networking companies, so you can prepare for interviews and negotiate from a position of knowledge. Since launch, engineers from 193 countries have visited the platform &mdash; from fresh graduates learning fiber basics to principal engineers designing transoceanic systems.</div>
    </div>
    <div class="faq-item">
        <div class="faq-q" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">What makes the MapYourTech books different from other optical networking books?<svg viewbox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><polyline points="6 9 12 15 18 9"></polyline></svg></div>
        <div class="faq-a">Most optical networking books are written by academics and lean heavily on theory &mdash; equations, proofs, and idealized scenarios that rarely match what you see in production. MapYourTech books are written by a practicing engineer with 18+ years of field experience across real operator networks. They focus on what you actually need on the job: how technologies behave in live deployments, what the real design trade-offs look like, which parameters matter when you are commissioning a link at 2 AM, and the practical skills that bridge the gap between textbook knowledge and production-ready engineering. These are the kind of insights that are hard to find anywhere &mdash; not in academic texts, not in vendor manuals, and certainly not from AI tools. Premium Pro members get access to the complete book library, including early access to future titles.</div>
    </div>

<script data-cfasync="false" src="/cdn-cgi/scripts/5c5dd728/cloudflare-static/email-decode.min.js"></script><script>
var annual = false;

function toggleBill() {
    annual = !annual;
    var t = document.getElementById('tgl');
    var m = document.getElementById('ml');
    var a = document.getElementById('al');
    if (annual) {
        t.classList.add('on');
        a.classList.add('active');
        m.classList.remove('active');
    } else {
        t.classList.remove('on');
        m.classList.add('active');
        a.classList.remove('active');
    }
    var els = document.querySelectorAll('.myt-pr-1740501000 .mp');
    var eas = document.querySelectorAll('.myt-pr-1740501000 .ap');
    for (var i = 0; i < els.length; i++) {
        els[i].setAttribute('style', annual ? 'display:none !important;' : '');
    }
    for (var i = 0; i < eas.length; i++) {
        eas[i].setAttribute('style', annual ? '' : 'display:none !important;');
    }
}

function toggleFaq(el) {
    var ans = el.nextElementSibling;
    var isOpen = ans.classList.contains('show');
    var allA = document.querySelectorAll('.myt-pr-1740501000 .faq-a');
    var allQ = document.querySelectorAll('.myt-pr-1740501000 .faq-q');
    for (var i = 0; i < allA.length; i++) {
        allA[i].classList.remove('show');
        allQ[i].classList.remove('open');
    }
    if (!isOpen) {
        ans.classList.add('show');
        el.classList.add('open');
    }
}
</script>

            // Fix login links
            const links = document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="login"], #loginpopup');
            links.forEach(function(link) {
                link.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    window.location.href = 'https://mapyourtech.com/login/';
                });
            });
            
            // Fix "Login here" text
            document.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(function(link) {
                if (link.textContent && link.textContent.toLowerCase().includes('login here')) {
                    link.href = 'https://mapyourtech.com/login/';
                }
            });
        });

            <script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        
        // Toast notification function
        function showToast(message, type) {
            type = type || 'info';
            
            // Remove existing toast
            var existingToast = document.querySelector('.myt-toast');
            if (existingToast) {
                existingToast.remove();
            }
            
            var toast = document.createElement('div');
            toast.className = 'myt-toast myt-toast-' + type;
            toast.textContent = message;
            document.body.appendChild(toast);
            
            setTimeout(function() {
                toast.classList.add('myt-toast-show');
            }, 10);
            
            setTimeout(function() {
                toast.classList.remove('myt-toast-show');
                setTimeout(function() {
                    toast.remove();
                }, 300);
            }, 3000);
        }
        
        // Like button functionality
        var likeButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.myt-like-button');
        
        likeButtons.forEach(function(button) {
            button.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                
                var postId = this.getAttribute('data-post-id');
                var countSpan = this.querySelector('.myt-like-count');
                var textSpan = this.querySelector('.myt-like-text');
                var heartIcon = this.querySelector('.myt-heart-icon');
                var btn = this;
                
                btn.classList.add('myt-animating');
                setTimeout(function() {
                    btn.classList.remove('myt-animating');
                }, 400);
                
                var formData = new FormData();
                formData.append('action', 'myt_toggle_like');
                formData.append('post_id', postId);
                formData.append('nonce', 'ee77064b9c');
                
                fetch('https://mapyourtech.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    body: formData,
                    credentials: 'same-origin'
                })
                .then(function(response) { return response.json(); })
                .then(function(data) {
                    if (data.success) {
                        countSpan.textContent = data.data.formatted;
                        
                        if (data.data.has_liked) {
                            btn.classList.add('myt-liked');
                            heartIcon.setAttribute('fill', 'currentColor');
                            btn.setAttribute('title', 'Remove from favorites');
                            if (textSpan) {
                                textSpan.textContent = data.data.is_logged_in ? 'Saved' : 'Liked';
                            }
                        } else {
                            btn.classList.remove('myt-liked');
                            heartIcon.setAttribute('fill', 'none');
                            btn.setAttribute('title', 'Add to favorites');
                            if (textSpan) {
                                textSpan.textContent = data.data.is_logged_in ? 'Save' : 'Like';
                            }
                        }
                        
                        if (data.data.message) {
                            showToast(data.data.message, data.data.has_liked ? 'success' : 'info');
                        }
                    }
                })
                .catch(function(error) {
                    console.error('Like error:', error);
                    showToast('Something went wrong. Please try again.', 'info');
                });
            });
        });
        
        // Remove favorite from list functionality
        var removeButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.myt-remove-favorite');
        
        removeButtons.forEach(function(button) {
            button.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                
                var postId = this.getAttribute('data-post-id');
                var item = this.closest('.myt-favorite-item');
                var btn = this;
                
                if (!confirm('Remove this article from your favorites?')) {
                    return;
                }
                
                var formData = new FormData();
                formData.append('action', 'myt_remove_favorite');
                formData.append('post_id', postId);
                formData.append('nonce', 'ee77064b9c');
                
                fetch('https://mapyourtech.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    body: formData,
                    credentials: 'same-origin'
                })
                .then(function(response) { return response.json(); })
                .then(function(data) {
                    if (data.success) {
                        item.style.opacity = '0';
                        item.style.transform = 'translateX(20px)';
                        
                        setTimeout(function() {
                            item.remove();
                            
                            // Update count
                            var countBadge = document.querySelector('.myt-favorites-count');
                            if (countBadge) {
                                var remaining = data.data.remaining;
                                countBadge.textContent = remaining + ' article' + (remaining !== 1 ? 's' : '');
                            }
                            
                            // Show empty state if no favorites left
                            if (data.data.remaining === 0) {
                                var container = document.querySelector('.myt-favorites-container');
                                if (container) {
                                    container.innerHTML = '<div class="myt-favorites-empty">' +
                                        '<div class="myt-fav-icon">💔</div>' +
                                        '<h3>No Favorites Yet</h3>' +
                                        '<p>You haven\'t saved any articles yet. Click the ❤️ heart button on any article to save it here!</p>' +
                                        '<a href="https://mapyourtech.com/blog/" class="myt-browse-btn">Browse Articles</a>' +
                                    '</div>';
                                }
                            }
                        }, 300);
                        
                        showToast('Removed from favorites', 'info');
                    }
                })
                .catch(function(error) {
                    console.error('Remove error:', error);
                    showToast('Something went wrong. Please try again.', 'info');
                });
            });
        });
    });
    </script>

		        <script type="text/javascript">
            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
                const loginPopup = document.getElementById('loginpopup');
                if (loginPopup) {
                    const newLoginPopup = loginPopup.cloneNode(true);
                    loginPopup.parentNode.replaceChild(newLoginPopup, loginPopup);

                    newLoginPopup.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
                        event.preventDefault();
                        event.stopImmediatePropagation();
                        window.location.href = 'https://mapyourtech.com/login';
                    });
                }
            });

            <script type="text/javascript">
    jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
        var checkCount = 0;
        var maxChecks = 20;
        
        function completelyHideDownloadButtons() {
            checkCount++;
            var hiddenButtons = 0;
            
            // Check for iframes
            $('iframe').each(function(index) {
                var iframe = this;
                
                try {
                    var iframeDoc = iframe.contentDocument || iframe.contentWindow.document;
                    if (iframeDoc) {
                        var $iframeDoc = $(iframeDoc);
                        
                        // Hide download/print buttons
                        $iframeDoc.find('button, a, input[type="button"], .btn, [role="button"]').each(function() {
                            var element = $(this);
                            var text = element.text().toLowerCase().trim();
                            var title = (element.attr('title') || '').toLowerCase();
                            var ariaLabel = (element.attr('aria-label') || '').toLowerCase();
                            
                            if (text.includes('download') || text.includes('print') || text.includes('save') ||
                                title.includes('download') || title.includes('print') || title.includes('save') ||
                                ariaLabel.includes('download') || ariaLabel.includes('print') || ariaLabel.includes('save')) {
                                
                                // Complete removal from view
                                element.css({
                                    'display': 'none',
                                    'visibility': 'hidden',
                                    'opacity': '0',
                                    'position': 'absolute',
                                    'left': '-9999px',
                                    'width': '0',
                                    'height': '0',
                                    'overflow': 'hidden',
                                    'pointer-events': 'none',
                                    'user-select': 'none'
                                });
                                
                                // Remove from accessibility tree
                                element.attr('aria-hidden', 'true');
                                element.attr('tabindex', '-1');
                                
                                // Disable all events
                                element.off();
                                element.on('click mousedown mouseup touchstart touchend', function(e) {
                                    e.preventDefault();
                                    e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                                    return false;
                                });
                                
                                hiddenButtons++;
                            }
                        });
                        
                        // Hide elements with download/print classes or IDs
                        $iframeDoc.find('[class*="download"], [id*="download"], [class*="print"], [id*="print"], [class*="save"], [id*="save"]').each(function() {
                            var element = $(this);
                            if (element.is(':visible')) {
                                element.css({
                                    'display': 'none',
                                    'visibility': 'hidden',
                                    'opacity': '0',
                                    'position': 'absolute',
                                    'left': '-9999px',
                                    'width': '0',
                                    'height': '0'
                                });
                                
                                element.attr('aria-hidden', 'true');
                                hiddenButtons++;
                            }
                        });
                        
                        // Special targeting for Font Awesome icons
                        $iframeDoc.find('.fa-download, .fa-print, .fa-save').each(function() {
                            var element = $(this);
                            element.css('display', 'none');
                            hiddenButtons++;
                        });
                    }
                } catch(e) {
                    console.log('Cannot access iframe ' + index + ':', e.message);
                }
            });
            
            // Also hide any download buttons on main page
            $('button, a, input[type="button"], .btn, [role="button"]').each(function() {
                var element = $(this);
                var text = element.text().toLowerCase().trim();
                var title = (element.attr('title') || '').toLowerCase();
                
                if ((text === 'download' || text === 'print' || text === 'save' ||
                     title === 'download' || title === 'print' || title === 'save') && 
                    element.is(':visible')) {
                    
                    element.css('display', 'none');
                    hiddenButtons++;
                }
            });
            
            if (hiddenButtons === 0 && checkCount < maxChecks) {
                setTimeout(completelyHideDownloadButtons, 1000);
            }
        }
        
        // Start after delay
        setTimeout(completelyHideDownloadButtons, 2000);
        
        // Monitor for new content
        var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
            mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
                if (mutation.addedNodes.length > 0) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < mutation.addedNodes.length; i++) {
                        var node = mutation.addedNodes[i];
                        if (node.nodeType === 1) {
                            var $node = $(node);
                            if ($node.is('iframe') || $node.find('iframe').length > 0) {
                                setTimeout(completelyHideDownloadButtons, 1000);
                                break;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        });
        
        observer.observe(document.body, {
            childList: true,
            subtree: true
        });
    });
    </script>

    <script>
    function showCoursePreview(courseId) {
        // Fetch course data via AJAX
        fetch('https://mapyourtech.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
            },
            body: 'action=get_course_preview&course_id=' + courseId + '&nonce=8e64696bfb'
        })
        .then(response => response.json())
        .then(data => {
            if (data.success) {
                document.getElementById('preview-title').textContent = data.data.title;
                document.getElementById('preview-subtitle').textContent = data.data.subtitle;
                document.getElementById('preview-description').innerHTML = data.data.description;
                
                // Populate lessons
                const lessonsList = document.getElementById('preview-lessons');
                lessonsList.innerHTML = '';
                data.data.lessons.forEach(lesson => {
                    const li = document.createElement('li');
                    li.className = 'lesson-item';
                    li.innerHTML = `
                        <span>${lesson.title}</span>
                        <span class="lesson-duration">${lesson.duration}</span>
                    `;
                    lessonsList.appendChild(li);
                });
                
                // Show modal
                document.getElementById('course-preview-modal').style.display = 'flex';
            }
        });
    }
    
    function closePreview() {
        document.getElementById('course-preview-modal').style.display = 'none';
    }
    
    function enrollInCourse() {
        // Implement enrollment logic
        alert('Enrollment feature coming soon!');
    }
    </script>
    			<script>
				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
			</script>

<script type="text/javascript">(function (undefined) {let scriptOptions={"_localizedStrings":{"redirect_overlay_title":"Hold On","redirect_overlay_text":"You are being redirected to another page,<br>it may take a few seconds.","webview_notification_text":"The selected provider doesn't support embedded browsers!"},"_targetWindow":"prefer-popup","_redirectOverlay":"overlay-with-spinner-and-message","_unsupportedWebviewBehavior":""};
/**
 * Used when Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy blocked the access to the opener. We can't have a reference of the opened windows, so we should attempt to refresh only the windows that has opened popups.
 */
window._nslHasOpenedPopup = false;
window._nslWebViewNoticeElement = null;

window.NSLPopup = function (url, title, w, h) {

    /**
     * Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy blocked the access to the opener
     */
    if (typeof BroadcastChannel === "function") {
        const _nslLoginBroadCastChannel = new BroadcastChannel('nsl_login_broadcast_channel');
        _nslLoginBroadCastChannel.onmessage = (event) => {
            if (window?._nslHasOpenedPopup && event.data?.action === 'redirect') {
                window._nslHasOpenedPopup = false;

                const url = event.data?.href;
                _nslLoginBroadCastChannel.close();
                if (typeof window.nslRedirect === 'function') {
                    window.nslRedirect(url);
                } else {
                    window.opener.location = url;
                }
            }
        };
    }

    const userAgent = navigator.userAgent,
        mobile = function () {
            return /\b(iPhone|iP[ao]d)/.test(userAgent) ||
                /\b(iP[ao]d)/.test(userAgent) ||
                /Android/i.test(userAgent) ||
                /Mobile/i.test(userAgent);
        },
        screenX = window.screenX !== undefined ? window.screenX : window.screenLeft,
        screenY = window.screenY !== undefined ? window.screenY : window.screenTop,
        outerWidth = window.outerWidth !== undefined ? window.outerWidth : document.documentElement.clientWidth,
        outerHeight = window.outerHeight !== undefined ? window.outerHeight : document.documentElement.clientHeight - 22,
        targetWidth = mobile() ? null : w,
        targetHeight = mobile() ? null : h,
        left = parseInt(screenX + (outerWidth - targetWidth) / 2, 10),
        right = parseInt(screenY + (outerHeight - targetHeight) / 2.5, 10),
        features = [];
    if (targetWidth !== null) {
        features.push('width=' + targetWidth);
    }
    if (targetHeight !== null) {
        features.push('height=' + targetHeight);
    }
    features.push('left=' + left);
    features.push('top=' + right);
    features.push('scrollbars=1');

    const newWindow = window.open(url, title, features.join(','));

    if (window.focus) {
        newWindow.focus();
    }

    window._nslHasOpenedPopup = true;

    return newWindow;
};

let isWebView = null;

function checkWebView() {
    if (isWebView === null) {
        function _detectOS(ua) {
            if (/Android/.test(ua)) {
                return "Android";
            } else if (/iPhone|iPad|iPod/.test(ua)) {
                return "iOS";
            } else if (/Windows/.test(ua)) {
                return "Windows";
            } else if (/Mac OS X/.test(ua)) {
                return "Mac";
            } else if (/CrOS/.test(ua)) {
                return "Chrome OS";
            } else if (/Firefox/.test(ua)) {
                return "Firefox OS";
            }
            return "";
        }

        function _detectBrowser(ua) {
            let android = /Android/.test(ua);

            if (/Opera Mini/.test(ua) || / OPR/.test(ua) || / OPT/.test(ua)) {
                return "Opera";
            } else if (/CriOS/.test(ua)) {
                return "Chrome for iOS";
            } else if (/Edge/.test(ua)) {
                return "Edge";
            } else if (android && /Silk\//.test(ua)) {
                return "Silk";
            } else if (/Chrome/.test(ua)) {
                return "Chrome";
            } else if (/Firefox/.test(ua)) {
                return "Firefox";
            } else if (android) {
                return "AOSP";
            } else if (/MSIE|Trident/.test(ua)) {
                return "IE";
            } else if (/Safari\//.test(ua)) {
                return "Safari";
            } else if (/AppleWebKit/.test(ua)) {
                return "WebKit";
            }
            return "";
        }

        function _detectBrowserVersion(ua, browser) {
            if (browser === "Opera") {
                return /Opera Mini/.test(ua) ? _getVersion(ua, "Opera Mini/") :
                    / OPR/.test(ua) ? _getVersion(ua, " OPR/") :
                        _getVersion(ua, " OPT/");
            } else if (browser === "Chrome for iOS") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "CriOS/");
            } else if (browser === "Edge") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "Edge/");
            } else if (browser === "Chrome") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "Chrome/");
            } else if (browser === "Firefox") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "Firefox/");
            } else if (browser === "Silk") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "Silk/");
            } else if (browser === "AOSP") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "Version/");
            } else if (browser === "IE") {
                return /IEMobile/.test(ua) ? _getVersion(ua, "IEMobile/") :
                    /MSIE/.test(ua) ? _getVersion(ua, "MSIE ")
                        :
                        _getVersion(ua, "rv:");
            } else if (browser === "Safari") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "Version/");
            } else if (browser === "WebKit") {
                return _getVersion(ua, "WebKit/");
            }
            return "0.0.0";
        }

        function _getVersion(ua, token) {
            try {
                return _normalizeSemverString(ua.split(token)[1].trim().split(/[^\w\.]/)[0]);
            } catch (o_O) {
            }
            return "0.0.0";
        }

        function _normalizeSemverString(version) {
            const ary = version.split(/[\._]/);
            return (parseInt(ary[0], 10) || 0) + "." +
                (parseInt(ary[1], 10) || 0) + "." +
                (parseInt(ary[2], 10) || 0);
        }

        function _isWebView(ua, os, browser, version, options) {
            switch (os + browser) {
                case "iOSSafari":
                    return false;
                case "iOSWebKit":
                    return _isWebView_iOS(options);
                case "AndroidAOSP":
                    return false;
                case "AndroidChrome":
                    return parseFloat(version) >= 42 ? /; wv/.test(ua) : /\d{2}\.0\.0/.test(version) ? true : _isWebView_Android(options);
            }
            return false;
        }

        function _isWebView_iOS(options) {
            const document = (window["document"] || {});

            if ("WEB_VIEW" in options) {
                return options["WEB_VIEW"];
            }
            return !("fullscreenEnabled" in document || "webkitFullscreenEnabled" in document || false);
        }

        function _isWebView_Android(options) {
            if ("WEB_VIEW" in options) {
                return options["WEB_VIEW"];
            }
            return !("requestFileSystem" in window || "webkitRequestFileSystem" in window || false);
        }

        const options = {},
            nav = window.navigator || {},
            ua = nav.userAgent || "",
            os = _detectOS(ua),
            browser = _detectBrowser(ua),
            browserVersion = _detectBrowserVersion(ua, browser);

        isWebView = _isWebView(ua, os, browser, browserVersion, options);
    }

    return isWebView;
}

function isAllowedWebViewForUserAgent(provider) {
    const facebookAllowedWebViews = [
        'Instagram',
        'FBAV',
        'FBAN'
    ];
    let whitelist = [];

    if (provider && provider === 'facebook') {
        whitelist = facebookAllowedWebViews;
    }

    const nav = window.navigator || {},
        ua = nav.userAgent || "";

    if (whitelist.length && ua.match(new RegExp(whitelist.join('|')))) {
        return true;
    }

    return false;
}

function disableButtonInWebView(providerButtonElement) {
    if (providerButtonElement) {
        providerButtonElement.classList.add('nsl-disabled-provider');
        providerButtonElement.setAttribute('href', '#');

        providerButtonElement.addEventListener('pointerdown', (e) => {
            if (!window._nslWebViewNoticeElement) {
                window._nslWebViewNoticeElement = document.createElement('div');
                window._nslWebViewNoticeElement.id = "nsl-notices-fallback";
                window._nslWebViewNoticeElement.addEventListener('pointerdown', function (e) {
                    this.parentNode.removeChild(this);
                    window._nslWebViewNoticeElement = null;
                });
                const webviewNoticeHTML = '<div class="error"><p>' + scriptOptions._localizedStrings.webview_notification_text + '</p></div>';

                window._nslWebViewNoticeElement.insertAdjacentHTML("afterbegin", webviewNoticeHTML);
                document.body.appendChild(window._nslWebViewNoticeElement);
            }
        });
    }

}

window._nslDOMReady(function () {

    window.nslRedirect = function (url) {
        if (scriptOptions._redirectOverlay) {
            const overlay = document.createElement('div');
            overlay.id = "nsl-redirect-overlay";
            let overlayHTML = '';
            const overlayContainer = "<div id='nsl-redirect-overlay-container'>",
                overlayContainerClose = "</div>",
                overlaySpinner = "<div id='nsl-redirect-overlay-spinner'></div>",
                overlayTitle = "<p id='nsl-redirect-overlay-title'>" + scriptOptions._localizedStrings.redirect_overlay_title + "</p>",
                overlayText = "<p id='nsl-redirect-overlay-text'>" + scriptOptions._localizedStrings.redirect_overlay_text + "</p>";

            switch (scriptOptions._redirectOverlay) {
                case "overlay-only":
                    break;
                case "overlay-with-spinner":
                    overlayHTML = overlayContainer + overlaySpinner + overlayContainerClose;
                    break;
                default:
                    overlayHTML = overlayContainer + overlaySpinner + overlayTitle + overlayText + overlayContainerClose;
                    break;
            }

            overlay.insertAdjacentHTML("afterbegin", overlayHTML);
            document.body.appendChild(overlay);
        }

        window.location = url;
    };

    let targetWindow = scriptOptions._targetWindow || 'prefer-popup',
        lastPopup = false;


    document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
        if (e.target) {
            const buttonLinkElement = e.target.closest('a[data-plugin="nsl"][data-action="connect"]') || e.target.closest('a[data-plugin="nsl"][data-action="link"]');
            if (buttonLinkElement) {
                if (lastPopup && !lastPopup.closed) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    lastPopup.focus();
                } else {

                    let href = buttonLinkElement.href,
                        success = false;
                    if (href.indexOf('?') !== -1) {
                        href += '&';
                    } else {
                        href += '?';
                    }

                    const redirectTo = buttonLinkElement.dataset.redirect;
                    if (redirectTo === 'current') {
                        href += 'redirect=' + encodeURIComponent(window.location.href) + '&';
                    } else if (redirectTo && redirectTo !== '') {
                        href += 'redirect=' + encodeURIComponent(redirectTo) + '&';
                    }

                    if (targetWindow !== 'prefer-same-window' && checkWebView()) {
                        targetWindow = 'prefer-same-window';
                    }

                    if (targetWindow === 'prefer-popup') {
                        lastPopup = NSLPopup(href + 'display=popup', 'nsl-social-connect', buttonLinkElement.dataset.popupwidth, buttonLinkElement.dataset.popupheight);
                        if (lastPopup) {
                            success = true;
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    } else if (targetWindow === 'prefer-new-tab') {
                        const newTab = window.open(href + 'display=popup', '_blank');
                        if (newTab) {
                            if (window.focus) {
                                newTab.focus();
                            }
                            success = true;
                            window._nslHasOpenedPopup = true;
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                    if (!success) {
                        window.location = href;
                        e.preventDefault();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    });

    let buttonCountChanged = false;

    const googleLoginButtons = document.querySelectorAll(' a[data-plugin="nsl"][data-provider="google"]');
    if (googleLoginButtons.length && checkWebView()) {
        googleLoginButtons.forEach(function (googleLoginButton) {
            if (scriptOptions._unsupportedWebviewBehavior === 'disable-button') {
                disableButtonInWebView(googleLoginButton);
            } else {
                googleLoginButton.remove();
                buttonCountChanged = true;
            }
        });
    }

    const facebookLoginButtons = document.querySelectorAll(' a[data-plugin="nsl"][data-provider="facebook"]');
    if (facebookLoginButtons.length && checkWebView() && /Android/.test(window.navigator.userAgent) && !isAllowedWebViewForUserAgent('facebook')) {
        facebookLoginButtons.forEach(function (facebookLoginButton) {
            if (scriptOptions._unsupportedWebviewBehavior === 'disable-button') {
                disableButtonInWebView(facebookLoginButton);
            } else {
                facebookLoginButton.remove();
                buttonCountChanged = true;
            }
        });
    }

    const separators = document.querySelectorAll('div.nsl-separator');
    if (buttonCountChanged && separators.length) {
        separators.forEach(function (separator) {
            const separatorParentNode = separator.parentNode;
            if (separatorParentNode) {
                const separatorButtonContainer = separatorParentNode.querySelector('div.nsl-container-buttons');
                if (separatorButtonContainer && !separatorButtonContainer.hasChildNodes()) {
                    separator.remove();
                }
            }
        })
    }

        jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
            setTimeout(function() {
                var el = $("#mapyourtech-welcome-overlay");
                if (el.length) {
                    el.addClass("show");
                    $("body").css("overflow", "hidden");

            function closeWelcome() {
                $("#mapyourtech-welcome-overlay").removeClass("show");
                $("body").css("overflow", "auto");
                $.post('https://mapyourtech.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
                    action: "dismiss_welcome",
                    nonce: "049f703fe9"
                }).fail(function() {
                    var expires = new Date();
                    expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                    document.cookie = "mapyourtech_welcome_shown=true;expires=" + expires.toUTCString() + ";path=/";
                });
            }
            
            $(document).on("click", ".myt-ws-close", function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                closeWelcome();
            });
            $(document).on("click", "#mapyourtech-welcome-overlay", function(e) {
                if (e.target === this) closeWelcome();
            });
            $(document).keydown(function(e) {
                if (e.key === "Escape") closeWelcome();
            });
            $(document).on("click", ".myt-ws-btn", function(e) {
                var href = $(this).attr("href");
                if (href && href !== "#") {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    closeWelcome();
                    setTimeout(function() { window.location.href = href; }, 300);
                }
            });
            
            // Auto-counting
            var counters = document.querySelectorAll('.myt-ws-counter');
            var counted = false;
            function animateCounters() {
                if (counted) return;
                counted = true;
                counters.forEach(function(counter) {
                    var target = parseInt(counter.getAttribute('data-target'));
                    var count = 0;
                    var increment = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(target / 55));
                    function updateCount() {
                        count += increment;
                        if (count >= target) { counter.textContent = target; }
                        else { counter.textContent = count; requestAnimationFrame(updateCount); }
                    }
                    updateCount();
                });
            }
            setTimeout(function() {
                if ($("#mapyourtech-welcome-overlay").hasClass("show")) animateCounters();
            }, 2400);
            
            setTimeout(function() {
                if ($("#mapyourtech-welcome-overlay").hasClass("show") && 
                    $("#mapyourtech-welcome-overlay").css("display") === "none") {
                    $("body").css("overflow", "auto");
                }
            }, 5000);
        });

        (function() {
            function getSessionId() {
                var sid = localStorage.getItem('myt_vt_sid');
                if (!sid) {
                    sid = 'sess_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9) + Date.now().toString(36);
                    localStorage.setItem('myt_vt_sid', sid);
                }
                return sid;
            }
            
            var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
            xhr.open('POST', 'https://mapyourtech.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', true);
            xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded');
            xhr.send(
                'action=myt_vt_track_page&' +
                'session_id=' + encodeURIComponent(getSessionId()) + '&' +
                'page_url=' + encodeURIComponent(window.location.href) + '&' +
                'page_title=' + encodeURIComponent(document.title) + '&' +
                'referrer=' + encodeURIComponent(document.referrer) + '&' +
                'user_id=0'
            );
        })();

                // Only if jQuery is available
                if (typeof jQuery === 'undefined') return;

                window.addEventListener('error', function(e) {
                    // Send to server to log
                    jQuery.ajax({
                        url: 'https://mapyourtech.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php',
                        type: 'POST',

                            lineno: e.lineno || 0,
                            colno: e.colno || 0,
                            url: window.location.href
                        },
                        // Don't show errors if logging fails
                        error: function() {}
                    });
                }, true);
            })();

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Add event listeners for all links with class 'pdf-link'
    const pdfLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.pdf-link');
    
    pdfLinks.forEach(function(link) {
        link.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
            // Prevent the default behavior (don't navigate away)
            event.preventDefault();
            
            const pdfUrl = link.getAttribute('href'); // Get the PDF URL from the link's href
            const iframeId = link.getAttribute('data-iframe-id'); // Get the iframe ID from the data attribute

            openPDF(pdfUrl, iframeId); // Open the PDF in the iframe
        });
    });
});

function openPDF(pdfUrl, iframeId) {
    // Add parameters to hide toolbar, navigation panes, and scrollbar
    const pdfUrlWithParams = pdfUrl + "#toolbar=0&navpanes=0&scrollbar=0"; // Disable toolbar and navigation panes

    // Set the iframe source to the PDF URL
    const iframe = document.getElementById(iframeId);
    iframe.src = pdfUrlWithParams; 

    // Show the iframe container
    document.getElementById(iframeId + '_container').style.display = 'block';
}

function closePDF(containerId) {
    // Hide the iframe container
    document.getElementById(containerId).style.display = 'none';
}


	
</script>
